<script type="text/ecmascript">
var SVG_IDX4_SVGRoot = null;
var SVG_IDX4_TrueCoords = null;
var SVG_IDX4_singleTip = null;
var SVG_IDX4_singleBox = null;
var SVG_IDX4_singleText = null;
var SVG_IDX4_tiptspan = null;
var SVG_IDX4_attrScale = 1;
var SVG_IDX4_rightEdge = null;
var SVG_IDX4_SVGHeight = null;
var SVG_IDX4_SVGWidth = null;
function SVG_IDX4_Init(anchor) {
   SVG_IDX4_SVGRoot = document.getElementById(anchor);
   SVG_IDX4_TrueCoords = SVG_IDX4_SVGRoot.createSVGPoint();
   SVG_IDX4_singleTip = document.getElementById(anchor + '_singleTip1');
   SVG_IDX4_singleBox = document.getElementById(anchor + '_singleBox1');
   SVG_IDX4_singleText = document.getElementById(anchor + '_singleText1');
   SVG_IDX4_tiptspan = document.getElementById(anchor + '_tiptspan1');
   SVG_IDX4_tiptspan.firstChild.nodeValue = null;
   SVG_IDX4_SVGRoot.addEventListener('mousemove', SVG_IDX4_ShowTooltip, false);
   SVG_IDX4_SVGRoot.addEventListener('mouseout', SVG_IDX4_HideTooltip, false);
   SVG_IDX4_SVGHeight = SVG_IDX4_SVGRoot.getAttributeNS(null, "height");
   SVG_IDX4_SVGWidth = SVG_IDX4_SVGRoot.getAttributeNS(null, "width");
   if (!isNaN(parseFloat(SVG_IDX4_SVGHeight)) && !isNaN(parseFloat(SVG_IDX4_SVGWidth)))
      SVG_IDX4_GetHW();
}
function SVG_IDX4_GetHW()
{
    if (SVG_IDX4_SVGWidth != null && SVG_IDX4_SVGWidth != "") {
       if (SVG_IDX4_SVGWidth.match(/%/)) {
          var factor = parseFloat(SVG_IDX4_SVGWidth.replace(/%/,""))/100;
          SVG_IDX4_SVGWidth = window.innerWidth * factor;
       }
       else if (SVG_IDX4_SVGWidth.match(/in/))
          SVG_IDX4_SVGWidth = parseFloat(SVG_IDX4_SVGWidth.replace(/in/,""))*96;
       else if (SVG_IDX4_SVGWidth.match(/cm/))
          SVG_IDX4_SVGWidth = parseFloat(SVG_IDX4_SVGWidth.replace(/in/,""))*96/2.54;
       else
           SVG_IDX4_SVGWidth = parseFloat(SVG_IDX4_SVGWidth);
    }
    if (SVG_IDX4_SVGHeight != null && SVG_IDX4_SVGHeight != "") {
       if (SVG_IDX4_SVGHeight.match(/%/)) {
          var factor = parseFloat(SVG_IDX4_SVGHeight.replace(/%/,""))/100;
          SVG_IDX4_SVGHeight = window.innerHeight * factor;
       }
       else if (SVG_IDX4_SVGHeight.match(/in/))
          SVG_IDX4_SVGHeight = parseFloat(SVG_IDX4_SVGHeight.replace(/in/,""))*96;
       else if (SVG_IDX4_SVGHeight.match(/cm/))
          SVG_IDX4_SVGHeight = parseFloat(SVG_IDX4_SVGHeight.replace(/in/,""))*96/2.54;
       else
           SVG_IDX4_SVGHeight = parseFloat(SVG_IDX4_SVGHeight);
    }
}
function SVG_IDX4_GetScaleFactors(evt)
{
   var zoomFactor = 1;
   windowWidth  = (top.innerWidth==undefined)  ? window.innerWidth  : top.innerWidth;
   windowHeight = (top.innerHeight==undefined) ? window.innerHeight : top.innerHeight;
   SVG_IDX4_rightEdge = (SVG_IDX4_SVGWidth) ? SVG_IDX4_SVGWidth - window.pageXOffset : windowWidth;
   if (parseFloat(SVG_IDX4_SVGWidth) > 0 || parseFloat(SVG_IDX4_SVGHeight) > 0)
      var tipScale = 1.875;
   else {
      var tipXScale  = (screen.width/windowWidth) / SVG_IDX4_SVGRoot.currentScale;
      var tipYScale  = (screen.height/windowHeight) / SVG_IDX4_SVGRoot.currentScale;
      var tipScale   = (tipXScale + tipYScale)/2.0;
   }
   SVG_IDX4_attrScale = tipScale;
   if (navigator.appName == 'Adobe SVG Viewer') {
      if (screen.deviceXDPI != null && screen.logicalXDPI != null)
         zoomFactor = screen.deviceXDPI/screen.logicalXDPI;
      SVG_IDX4_attrScale = zoomFactor*tipScale;
   }
   else if (navigator.userAgent != null && navigator.userAgent != '') {
      var ua = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
      if (ua.indexOf("msie") != -1 || ua.indexOf("trident") != -1) {
         zoomFactor = screen.deviceXDPI/screen.logicalXDPI;
         SVG_IDX4_attrScale = tipScale/zoomFactor;
         SVG_IDX4_rightEdge /= zoomFactor;
      }
      else if (ua.indexOf("ipad") != -1) {
         zoomFactor = SVG_IDX4_SVGRoot.clientWidth / window.innerWidth;
         SVG_IDX4_attrScale = 1.5 / zoomFactor;
         SVG_IDX4_rightEdge /= zoomFactor;
      }
      else if (ua.indexOf("opera") != -1)
         SVG_IDX4_attrScale = tipScale;
      else if (ua.indexOf("firefox") != -1)
         SVG_IDX4_attrScale = tipScale;
      else {
         if (SVG_IDX4_SVGWidth > 0 || SVG_IDX4_SVGHeight > 0)
            zoomFactor = 1;
         else
            zoomFactor = parseInt(document.defaultView.getComputedStyle(SVG_IDX4_SVGRoot, null).width,10)/
                                  SVG_IDX4_SVGRoot.clientWidth;
         SVG_IDX4_attrScale = tipScale/zoomFactor;
         SVG_IDX4_rightEdge *= zoomFactor;
      }
   }
}
function SVG_IDX4_GetTrueCoords(evt)
{
   var trans = SVG_IDX4_SVGRoot.currentTranslate;
   var scale = SVG_IDX4_SVGRoot.currentScale;
   SVG_IDX4_GetScaleFactors();
   var p1    = SVG_IDX4_SVGRoot.createSVGPoint();
   var p2;
      var m = SVG_IDX4_SVGRoot.getScreenCTM();
      if (navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().indexOf("ipad") != -1) {
         p1.x = evt.clientX + window.pageXOffset;
         p1.y = evt.clientY + window.pageYOffset;
      }
      else {
      p1.x = evt.clientX;
      p1.y = evt.clientY;
      }
      p2 = p1.matrixTransform(m.inverse());
   SVG_IDX4_TrueCoords.x = Math.round(p2.x*100) / 100;
   SVG_IDX4_TrueCoords.y = Math.round(p2.y*100) / 100;
}
function SVG_IDX4_HideTooltip( evt )
{
   SVG_IDX4_tiptspan.firstChild.nodeValue = null;
   SVG_IDX4_singleTip.setAttributeNS(null, 'visibility', 'hidden');
}
function SVG_IDX4_ShowTooltip( evt )
{
   SVG_IDX4_GetTrueCoords( evt );
   var targetElement = evt.target;
   var tspanCount = targetElement.getElementsByTagName('desc').length;
   if (tspanCount == 1) {
      var targetTspan = targetElement.getElementsByTagName('desc').item(0);
      if ( targetTspan) {
         if (targetTspan.firstChild != null)
            SVG_IDX4_tiptspan.firstChild.nodeValue = targetTspan.firstChild.nodeValue; }
   }
   if ( '' != SVG_IDX4_tiptspan.firstChild.nodeValue )
   {
      var outline = SVG_IDX4_singleText.getBBox();
      SVG_IDX4_singleBox.setAttributeNS(null, 'transform', 'scale(' + SVG_IDX4_attrScale + ',' + SVG_IDX4_attrScale + ')' );
      SVG_IDX4_singleText.setAttributeNS(null, 'transform', 'scale(' + SVG_IDX4_attrScale + ',' + SVG_IDX4_attrScale + ')' );
      SVG_IDX4_singleTip.setAttributeNS(null, 'visibility', 'visible');
      if (evt.clientX + ((outline.width + 8)/0.8) * SVG_IDX4_attrScale > SVG_IDX4_rightEdge) {
         var xPos = SVG_IDX4_TrueCoords.x - parseInt((outline.width + 8)*SVG_IDX4_attrScale);
         if (xPos < 0)
            xPos = 0;
      }
      else
         var xPos = SVG_IDX4_TrueCoords.x;
      if (SVG_IDX4_TrueCoords.y < 16) {
         var yPos = SVG_IDX4_TrueCoords.y + ((outline.height + 16)/0.8)*SVG_IDX4_attrScale;
         if (yPos > windowHeight)
            yPos = SVG_IDX4_TrueCoords.y - parseInt((outline.height + 8)*SVG_IDX4_attrScale);
      }
      else
         var yPos = SVG_IDX4_TrueCoords.y - parseInt((outline.height + 8)*SVG_IDX4_attrScale);
      if (Number(outline.width == 0))
         SVG_IDX4_singleBox.setAttributeNS(null, 'width', outline.width);
      else
         SVG_IDX4_singleBox.setAttributeNS(null, 'width', outline.width + 8);
      SVG_IDX4_singleBox.setAttributeNS(null, 'height', outline.height + 8);
      SVG_IDX4_singleTip.setAttributeNS(null, 'transform', 'translate(' + xPos + ',' + yPos + ')');
   }
}

<p class="c proctitle">í‘œë³¸ í¬ê¸° = 46</p>
</div>

### EXAMPLE 10.13


```python
%%SAS

ods graphics off;ods exclude all;ods noresults;
PROC ANOVA DATA=exam_10_1;
	CLASS diet;
	MODEL weight=diet;
	MEANS diet/  hovtest= bartlett;
	ods output Bartlett=Bartlett;
RUN;
ods graphics on;ods exclude none;ods results;
PROC PRINT DATA=Bartlett;
RUN;
```

### EXAMPLE 10.14


```python
%%SAS

PROC IML;
n={5, 5, 4, 5};
v={4, 4, 3, 4};
v_a={0.0518, 0.0597, 0.0465, 0.0456};
sum_v=sum(v);
sum_vv=sum(v#v_a);
v_p=sum_vv/sum_v;
v_p2=(v_p)**2;
sum_vv2=sum((v#v_a)#v_a);
chi_stat=round((sum_vv2-(((sum_vv)**2)/sum_v))/(v_p2*(0.5+v_p2)), 0.001);
chi_crit=round(abs(quantile("chisq", 1-0.05, 3)), 0.001);
PRINT sum_v sum_vv v_p v_p2 sum_vv2 chi_stat chi_crit;
RUN;
QUIT;
```
